                      <div data-reactid="317">
                       GLAMPING in LA -Nature! Private Garden Art-Studio Space with your own little bar &amp; breakfast table under the trees. The Space is part of our Artist Community &amp; has 2 beds &amp; is just steps away from main house with 3 bathrooms &amp; Community Kitchen .
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="318">
                       This awesome Artist Hideaway Garden Cottage sits on a large 17,000 sqft Artist Live/ Work property with huge trees and a wild , campground style feel . Your garden studio comes with a free fresh fruit basket and some snacks and fresh filtered Alkaline Water. Everyone on the property loves to focus on what brings us together as human beings instead of what divides us. By renting your private garden cottage with us, you rent more than just a room in a boring house in a big city! You will live in a fun, cool, hip creative space with access to a 17,000 sqft big creative park like yard space with huge trees and lots of places to be creative and inspired in ! Perfect for people who love to create and build things or just chill under a tree in our park like setting lounging on one of the outdoor couches and just About our space: Our space is wired with super High Speed Internet (75 Mbps) Since our garden space is like our preferred living room, its also the place where most of our socializing happens. There is also a large big screen TV Outdoor Theater Space OUTSIDE under the trees with 2 couches where you have access to ATT fiber optic U-Verse Family TV Channel Amazon Prime Movies and Hulu , So grab your blankets and settle down and take in a movie under the stars on one of our couches or on our good size lawn space to put your blanket or chair . While we do our best to ensure that your space is clean and sanitary, please keep in mind that here we live in HARMONY with nature, so if your someone who is afraid of a little cricket or a little bug sharing our yard, this might not be the best place for you! Our common outdoor living spaces also include a large oak garden workstation table ( our "internet cafee" ) for group work, gatherings or meetings with internet/ electric hook up . Washer / Dryer, Extended outdoor kitchen with outdoor dining table, Gas BBQ grill and 3 different table areas to enjoy your breakfast outdoors or just work away on your laptop. Trampoline, outdoor couches with tiki lamps , pond with small waterfall, a cool Gazebo to hang out in the shade and a TIKI BAR ! Whats included: when renting with us you have access to our "Open Community Kitchen" where you can find the basic spices, pots and pans, some basic staple foods and organic fruits and veggies which are included in your rent because we like to share our food.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="319">
                       short walk to metro link, 20 + restaurants and lots of stores and Reseda parks wonderful lake where you can feed the ducks and relax by the water 3 great Thai restaurants within walking distance, 2 Persian food buffets which are amazing, many more international restaurants we have not tried yet ,and crazy good PHO places and a vegetarian chinese restaurant all withing walking distance. . ..and Subway is open 24 hours and we have a drive-in starbucks which opens at 4:30am just 1 block away . . ..and we also have way to many fast food/ restaurants and 7/11's right within just a couple blocks of our beautiful campground kind of haven ! Also, a big bonus, we live half a block from the very dried up LA river and Reseda park and rec center where you can find ducks and awesome late night Taco trucks and for those who fear, we live 2 blocks away from police station , we are also only 8 minutes away from Balboa park, the Archery range, 2 golf courses, basket ball and tennis courts and all the more upscale stuff Encino ,Tarzana and Northridge has to offer we also have the metro link right down a couple blocks where you can hop on the train and end up in NoHo / studio city in no time. . .. Many of us moved here from Santa Monica and never realized how much more cool stuff there is and how many good places there are to shop and eat . . .. Our Park-like setting feels like a remote area , but rest assured your right in the middle of everything . Its the perfect place to be relaxing in the middle of everything in your nature retreat with huge trees and fun people and a good creative vibe.

                      <div data-reactid="1942">
                       A beautiful private cottage surrounded by a babbling brook. The property is on a 3+ acre farm with an alpaca, pony, goats and birds of all kinds. There are two private patios to enjoy. Full kitchen, living room and bath and a King bed.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1943">
                       A beautiful private cottage with a wood-burning fireplace in the open plan sitting-room complete with a reading library and eat-in kitchen. A bright bathroom with tub/shower and a large cozy bedroom with a king size bed will make you feel right at home. Two private patios with seating invite you to relax and enjoy the babbling stream. The surrounding property is a little farm where miniature goats, miniature ponies, alpacas and many other animals. Ducks, birds and chickens (no roosters!) roam the property and the large pond adjacent to the cottage is full of beautiful koi fish and turtles.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1944">
                       We are conveniently located near Ventura Boulevard which has access to everything you might need: lots of great stores, salons, markets, cafes and restaurants. We are a just a few miles from the Santa Monica mountains which has beautiful hiking trails. There are many fabulous beaches within easy travel distance. Or like many you just may want to enjoy being here!

                     <div data-reactid="2069">
                      <div data-reactid="2070">
                       This quiet house with private patio + entrance is the perfect place to relax. This one bedroom house includes dining area with small office nook, fully equipped kitchen and living room. Bedroom and bathroom are separated by door from main living area.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2071">
                       This 500 sq. ft. (47 m²) spacious, open, and newly furnished one-bed room guest house is located behind our main house (separate dwelling), with private entrance through alley. Easy ample street parking with no restrictions. There are hard wood floors throughout the house with AC &amp; Heat. The LIVING ROOM w/ OPEN KITCHEN is bright and airy. The front door and main windows face the back of the property/alley. Kitchen includes stove-top (no oven), microwave, toaster oven, coffee press + machine, tea pot and full-sized fridge. Kitchen is fully equipped with pretty much everything you have at home – if something is missing, we can help. Dish soap, paper towels, trash bags and kitchen towels are provided for your stay. In addition to dining table, there is a small office nook for your laptop (wifi provided). 47' wall-mounted flat screen TV provides access to DirecTV and DVD player. New comfortable couch w/ leg rest will help you relax in the evenings. The PATIO features a wooden table with two benches for private breakfasts and two new lounge chairs with foot stools for drinks at night. Area is covered with sun sails. The BEDROOM comfortably accommodates two guests who travel together or separate (two separate full-size beds which can be pushed together). There is plenty of built-in closet, space and storage area. The BATHROOM has a shower. We provide cotton towels, toilet paper, shampoo/conditioner and soap for the fully-tiled, cozy bathroom. Laundry is on-site and can be used on occasion. 2 person maximum occupancy (adults only, no small kids – no exceptions). No pets of any kind (no exceptions). No visitors without permission. Smoking is allowed anywhere outside of the house.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2072">
                       We are located in the Valley of Los Angeles, a 30 min drive (15 miles) from Santa Monica and 20 min drive (13 miles) from Hollywood. Lake Balboa is a residential, family-oriented and safe neighborhood. Take a stroll Sunday morning down to the local Encino Farmer's Market to stock up on fresh, organic fruits &amp; veggies or rent a bike (or boat) at Lake Balboa. Play a round of golf at one of the three nearby golf courses. Grab your racket for a tennis game. Enjoy the nearby Japanese Gardens. There is so much to do and explore in this area! Lake Balboa is the perfect location for traveling all over LA and beyond. Take a day trip to the Santa Barbara wineries, hop "over the hill" on one of the beautiful canyon roads and end up in Hollywood, Beverly Hills, Santa Monica, or Malibu in no time! Get tickets to a show at the Hollywood Bowl and enjoy a concert and picnic under the infamous Hollywood sign. Hike one of the many beautiful canyon trails. Tour the Malibu wineries. Visit local breweries. Spend the day at one of our many beaches. Tour the studios. Reserve tickets to a taping (email hidden) show. Experience all the amazing restaurants LA has to offer. Convenient for college sports fans to catch a USC or UCLA game live. Explore all the wonderful museums or walking tours in our historic city. Need a suggestion? Feel free to ask me! Convenient to three Targets, many grocery stores (Trader Joe's, Whole Foods, Gelson's, Ralph's, Von's, various ethnic markets, and more), pharmacies (CVS, Walgreens, Rite Aid), and restaurants (fine dining, casual, take-out).
